<span data-ttu-id="1ba7c-1231">Cette classe contient les attributs suivants pour Windows Server 2012 :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1ba7c-1231">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
